## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  A[modifyDwellNotification(locationCode, recipients)] --> B[filter recipients where status not null]
  B --> C{recipient.status === "deleted"}
  C -->|yes| D[map -> {id, status}]
  C -->|no| E[map -> full recipient payload (id, location_code, name, shift_start, shift_end, alert_level, phone_number, status)]
  D --> F[requestConfig.data.recipients]
  E --> F
  F --> G[requestConfig: { method: "POST", data }]
  G --> H[modifyDwellDuck.fetch(CONFIGURE_DWELL_NOTIFICATION_URL, requestConfig)]
  H --> I[dispatch(fetch action)]
  I --> J[returns promise of API response]
```

> SVG rendering failed for this diagram.

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant Caller
  participant ActionCreator as modifyDwellNotification
  participant Dispatcher as dispatch
  participant Duck as modifyDwellDuck
  Caller->>ActionCreator: invoke with locationCode, recipients
  ActionCreator->>Dispatcher: build requestConfig and call modifyDwellDuck.fetch(url, config)
  Dispatcher->>Duck: execute fetch
  Duck-->>Dispatcher: fetch promise
  Dispatcher-->>Caller: returns promise
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> BuildingRequest: invoked
  BuildingRequest --> Fetching: dispatch fetch
  Fetching --> Success: API returns success
  Fetching --> Failure: API returns error
  Success --> Idle
  Failure --> Idle
```
